RESUMO 

  O presente estudo tem como objetivo verificar em que medida as quest√µes do Exame

ENEM √† luz das compet√™ncias e habilidades previstas na BNCC; e iii) apresentar a classifica√ß√£o 

das quest√µes do ENEM de 2014 a 2018 por meio de gr√°ficos e tabelas. Para isso utilizou-se 

como metodologia a pesquisa documental, analisando as compet√™ncias e habilidades previstas

ABSTRACT 

  The present study aims to verify to what extent the questions of the Exame Nacional do Ensino 
M√©dio of the last five years (2014‚Äì2018) contemplate the guidelines (skills and competences) 
of the Base Nacional Comum, and as specific objectives: i) to describe the reference matrix of 
the Exame Nacional do Ensino M√©dio; ii) to analyze the questions of the Exame Nacional do 
Ensino M√©dio in the light of the competences and abilities provided for in the Base Nacional 
Comum Curricular; and iii) present the classification of the questions of the Exame Nacional 
do Ensino M√©dio from 2014 to 2018 through graphs and tables. For this, we use as methodology 
a  documentary  research,  analyzing  the  competences  and  abilities  foreseen  in  the  BNCC  and 
classifying 
2018.  
As a result, there are still some shortcomings between the ENEM test in relation to BNCC skills 
and competences, as there  is a certain  imbalance in the  frequency of  items that work certain 
competencies.
